  <script type="text/javascript">
    (function() {
        var contextPath = '/jira';
        var eventBuffer = [];

        function printDeprecatedMsg() {
            if (console && console.warn) {
                console.warn('DEPRECATED JS - contextPath global variable has been deprecated since 7.4.0. Use `wrm/context-path` module instead.');
            }
        }

        function sendEvent(analytics, postfix) {
            analytics.send({
                name: 'js.globals.contextPath.' + postfix
            });
        }

        function sendDeprecatedEvent(postfix) {
            try {
                var analytics = require('jira/analytics');
                if (eventBuffer.length) {
                    eventBuffer.forEach(function(value) {
                        sendEvent(analytics, value);
                    });
                    eventBuffer = [];
                }

                if (postfix) {
                    sendEvent(analytics, postfix);
                }
            } catch(ex) {
                eventBuffer.push(postfix);
                setTimeout(sendDeprecatedEvent, 1000);
            }
        }

        Object.defineProperty(window, 'contextPath', {
            get: function() {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('get');
                return contextPath;
            },
            set: function(value) {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('set');
                contextPath = value;
            }
        });
    })();

</script>

              <div id="descriptionmodule" class="module toggle-wrap">
               <div id="descriptionmodule_heading" class="mod-header">
                <ul class="ops"></ul>
                <h2 class="toggle-title">Description</h2>
               </div>
               <div class="mod-content">
                <div id="description-val" class="field-ignore-highlight"> 
                 <div class="user-content-block"> 
                  <p>Problem doing a delta-import such that records marked as "deleted" in the database are removed from Solr using deletedPkQuery.</p> 
                  <p>Here's a config I'm using against a mocked test database:</p> 
                  <div class="code panel" style="border-width: 1px;">
                   <div class="codeContent panelContent"> 
                    <pre class="code-xml"><span class="code-tag">&lt;dataConfig&gt;</span>
 <span class="code-tag">&lt;dataSource driver=<span class="code-quote">"com.mysql.jdbc.Driver"</span> url=<span class="code-quote">"jdbc:mysql://localhost/db"</span>/&gt;</span>
 <span class="code-tag">&lt;document name=<span class="code-quote">"tests"</span>&gt;</span>
   &lt;entity name=<span class="code-quote">"test"</span>
           pk=<span class="code-quote">"board_id"</span>
           transformer=<span class="code-quote">"TemplateTransformer"</span>
           deletedPkQuery=<span class="code-quote">"select board_id from boards where deleted = <span class="code-quote">'Y'</span>"</span>
           query=<span class="code-quote">"select * from boards where deleted = <span class="code-quote">'N'</span>"</span>
           deltaImportQuery=<span class="code-quote">"select * from boards where deleted = <span class="code-quote">'N'</span>"</span>
           deltaQuery=<span class="code-quote">"select * from boards where deleted = <span class="code-quote">'N'</span>"</span>
           preImportDeleteQuery=<span class="code-quote">"datasource:board"</span>&gt;
     <span class="code-tag">&lt;field column=<span class="code-quote">"id"</span> template=<span class="code-quote">"board-${test.board_id}"</span>/&gt;</span>
     <span class="code-tag">&lt;field column=<span class="code-quote">"datasource"</span> template=<span class="code-quote">"board"</span>/&gt;</span>
     <span class="code-tag">&lt;field column=<span class="code-quote">"title"</span> /&gt;</span>
   <span class="code-tag">&lt;/entity&gt;</span>
 <span class="code-tag">&lt;/document&gt;</span>
<span class="code-tag">&lt;/dataConfig&gt;</span>
</pre> 
                   </div>
                  </div> 
                  <p>Note that the uniqueKey in Solr is the "id" field. And its value is a template board-&lt;PK&gt;.</p> 
                  <p>I noticed the javadoc comments in DocBuilder#collectDelta it says "Note: In our definition, unique key of Solr document is the primary key of the top level entity". This of course isn't really an appropriate assumption.</p> 
                 </div> 
                </div> 
               </div>
              </div>

\u003cspan class=\'commentdate_12722427_verbose subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'21\\/Jun\\/09 21:11\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2009-06-21T21:11:20+0000\'\u003e21\\/Jun\\/09 21:11\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e  \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eThere are two bugs in this issue:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e1) The deletedPkQuery must say \\\"select field from table\\\". It may not say \\\"select expression\\\" or \\\"select field AS FIELD from table\\\". The former does not work and the latter may work with some databases and not others.  In other words, the first example works and the others fail:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e    deletedPkQuery=\\\"select id from item where EXPRESSION\\\"\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n    deletedPkQuery=\\\"select concat(\'\',id) from item where EXPRESSION\\\"\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n    deletedPkQuery=\\\"select id from item AS ID where EXPRESSION\\\"\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n    deletedPkQuery=\\\"select id from item AS ITEM.ID where EXPRESSION\\\"\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e2) If a template is used to format the contents of the Solr primary key, that template is declared at the &lt;field&gt; level and is not visible in the parent &lt;entity&gt; level. Since the deletedPkQuery is declared in the &lt;entity&gt; level, it cannot see the field\'s template. Thus the template cannot be applied to the results of the deletedPkQuery. Any formatting in the &lt;field&gt; template must be duplicated (in SQL syntax) in the deletedPkQuery. \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThis is workaround that achieves the goal of #2: if the Solr primary key is declared as\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e    &lt;field name=\\\"id\\\" template=\\\"prefix-${item.id}\\\"\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003ethen the deletedPkQuery must be declared as\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e    deletedPkQuery=\\\"select concat(\'prefix\',id) from item where EXPRESSION\\\"\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eBecause of bug #1, it is not possible to use this workaround.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe attached patch fixes bug #1, making it possible to use the workaround. It is Erik\'s second patch but only with the fix for bug #1. In other words, the first example works and the others fail: \\n\\n     deletedPkQuery=\\\"select id from item where EXPRESSION\\\" \\n    deletedPkQuery=\\\"select concat(\'\',id) from item where EXPRESSION\\\" \\n    deletedPkQuery=\\\"select id from item AS ID where EXPRESSION\\\" \\n    deletedPkQuery=\\\"select id from item AS ITEM.ID where EXPRESSION\\\" \\n\\n 2) If a template is used to format the contents of the Solr primary key, that template is declared at the &lt;field&gt; level and is not visible in the parent &lt;entity&gt; level. It is Erik\'s second patch but only with the fix for bug #1. always be the Solr name, and if it is a templated field, it should be \'name\'\\/\'template\' not \'column\'\\/\'template\', for example.    \\n             \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_12724471_verbose subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'26\\/Jun\\/09 10:58\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2009-06-26T10:58:33+0000\'\u003e26\\/Jun\\/09 10:58\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e  \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eErik, the most common use-case as far as I have seen is that the primary key in tables is different from the uniqueKey in Solr (think about multiple tables with each having a root-entity). Yes, the pk can be transformed (or one can alias it in sql) but this being the most common use-case, I feel pk should be kept as-is.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eLet me give a few possible cases \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\u003col\u003e\\n\\t\u003cli\u003eThe name of table\'s primary key is different from solr\'s unique key name and the deletedPkQuery returns only one column (most common use-case)\u003c\\/li\u003e\\n\\t\u003cli\u003eThe name of table\'s primary key is different from solr\'s unique key name and the deletedPkQuery returns multiple columns\u003c\\/li\u003e\\n\\t\u003cli\u003eThe name of table\'s primary key is same as solr\'s unique key name and the deletedPkQuery returns only one column\u003c\\/li\u003e\\n\\t\u003cli\u003eThe name of table\'s primary key is same as solr\'s unique key name and the deletedPkQuery returns multiple columns\u003c\\/li\u003e\\n\u003c\\/ol\u003e\\n\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eFor #1 \'pk\' does not matter because we can use the single columns coming back from deletedPkQuery\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nFor #2, \'pk\' is required otherwise the user is forced to use a transformer (or alias). For non-database use-cases (there is none right now), there is no aliasing so the user must write a transformer\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nFor #3, neither \'pk\' nor \'uniqueKey\' matters\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nFor #4, we can use solr\'s uniqueKey name (I guess this is your use-case?). I think that this is a rare use-case.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eIf at all, we decide to go with uniqueKey only, the right way to do that would be to use the corresponding column-mapping for looking up the unique key. For the example below, we should use \\\"db-id\\\" to lookup in the map returned by deletedPkQuery if solr-id is the uniqueKey in solr:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\u003cdiv class=\\\"code panel\\\" style=\\\"border-width: 1px;\\\"\u003e\u003cdiv class=\\\"codeContent panelContent\\\"\u003e\\n\u003cpre class=\\\"code-xml\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"code-tag\\\"\u003e&lt;field column=\u003cspan class=\\\"code-quote\\\"\u003e\\\"db-id\\\"\u003c\\/span\u003e name=\u003cspan class=\\\"code-quote\\\"\u003e\\\"solr-id\\\"\u003c\\/span\u003e \\/&gt;\u003c\\/span\u003e\\n\u003c\\/pre\u003e\\n\u003c\\/div\u003e\u003c\\/div\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eHowever, even though the above approach is the \'right\' one, it is very tricky and hard to explain to users. Also, there could be multiple columns mapped to same solr key (think about template for unique key for \'types\' of documents based on a flag column). This may be very error-prone.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eWhat do you think?\u003c\\/p\u003e \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Expand comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-collapsed\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eShow\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details flooded\\\"\u003e\\n                        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"shalinmangar\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_12724471_concise\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=shalinmangar\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"shalinmangar\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Shalin Shekhar Mangar\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_12724471_concise subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'26\\/Jun\\/09 10:58\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2009-06-26T10:58:33+0000\'\u003e26\\/Jun\\/09 10:58\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e                    Erik, the most common use-case as far as I have seen is that the primary key in tables is different from the uniqueKey in Solr (think about multiple tables with each having a root-entity). Yes, the pk can be transformed (or one can alias it in sql) but this being the most common use-case, I feel pk should be kept as-is. \\n\\n Let me give a few possible cases  \\n \\n\\t The name of table\'s primary key is different from solr\'s unique key name and the deletedPkQuery returns only one column (most common use-case) \\n\\t The name of table\'s primary key is different from solr\'s unique key name and the deletedPkQuery returns multiple columns \\n\\t The name of table\'s primary key is same as solr\'s unique key name and the deletedPkQuery returns only one column \\n\\t The name of table\'s primary key is same as solr\'s unique key name and the deletedPkQuery returns multiple columns \\n \\n\\n\\n For #1 \'pk\' does not matter because we can use the single columns coming back from deletedPkQuery \\nFor #2, \'pk\' is required otherwise the user is forced to use a transformer (or alias). For non-database use-cases (there is none right now), there is no aliasing so the user must write a transformer \\nFor #3, neither \'pk\' nor \'uniqueKey\' matters \\nFor #4, we can use solr\'s uniqueKey name (I guess this is your use-case?). I think that this is a rare use-case. \\n\\n If at all, we decide to go with uniqueKey only, the right way to do that would be to use the corresponding column-mapping for looking up the unique key. For the example below, we should use \\\"db-id\\\" to lookup in the map returned by deletedPkQuery if solr-id is the uniqueKey in solr: \\n  \\n  &lt;field column= \\\"db-id\\\"  name= \\\"solr-id\\\"  \\/&gt; \\n \\n  \\n\\n However, even though the above approach is the \'right\' one, it is very tricky and hard to explain to users. Also, there could be multiple columns mapped to same solr key (think about template for unique key for \'types\' of documents based on a flag column). This may be very error-prone. \\n\\n What do you think?              \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n\u003c\\/div\u003e\\n                             \\n\\n\\n\u003cdiv id=\\\"comment-12724780\\\" class=\\\"issue-data-block activity-comment twixi-block  expanded\\\"\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap verbose actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Collapse comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-expanded\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eHide\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-links\\\"\u003e\\n                \u003ca href=\\\"\\/jira\\/browse\\/SOLR-1229?focusedCommentId=12724780&page=com.atlassian.jira.plugin.system.issuetabpanels:comment-tabpanel#comment-12724780\\\"\\n                   title=\\\"Right click and copy link for a permanent link to this comment.\\\" class=\\\"activitymodule-link issue-comment-action\\\"\u003e\\n                    \u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-link\\\"\u003ePermalink\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n                                            \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details\\\"\u003e        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"ehatcher\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_12724780_verbose\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=ehatcher\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"ehatcher\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Erik Hatcher\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eAlso, I recommend that a feature be removed: creating a deltaImportQuery if the user does not declare one. From the wiki:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e\\\"deltaImportQuery : (Only used in delta-import) . If this is not present , DIH tries to construct the import query by(after identifying the delta) modifying the \'query\' (this is error prone). There is a namespace ${dataimporter.delta.&lt;column-name&gt;} which can be used in this query. e.g: select * from tbl where id=${dataimporter.delta.id}   Solr1.4.\\\"\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe user should just be required to supply the deltaImportQuery. Now that the deltaImportQuery declaration exists, this \\\"helper feature\\\" is just a trap for the unwary.
